<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">About</h2><a id="user-content-about" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: About" href="#about"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://ce.judge0.com" rel="nofollow">Judge0</a> (pronounced like "judge zero") is a robust, scalable, and <a href="https://github.com/judge0/judge0">open-source</a> <strong>online code execution system</strong>. You can use it to build a wide range of applications that need online code execution features. Some examples include competitive programming platforms, e-learning platforms, candidate assessment and recruitment platforms, online code editors, online IDEs, and many more.</p>
<p dir="auto">In our research paper <a href="https://paper.judge0.com" rel="nofollow">Robust and Scalable Online Code Execution System</a>, we present Judge0's modern modular architecture that can be easily deployed and scaled. We study its design, comment on the various challenges in building such systems, and compare it with other available online code execution systems and online judge systems.</p>
<p dir="auto">To see Judge0 in action, try <a href="https://ide.judge0.com" rel="nofollow">Judge0 IDE</a> - our free and open-source online code editor.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Quick and easy <a href="https://judge0.com/#pricing" rel="nofollow">installation</a></li>
<li>Rich and verbose <a href="https://ce.judge0.com" rel="nofollow">API documentation</a></li>
<li>Scalable architecture</li>
<li>Sandboxed compilation and execution</li>
<li>Support for <a href="#supported-languages">60+ languages</a></li>
<li>Compilation and execution of multi-file programs</li>
<li>Support for additional files alongside the user's program</li>
<li>Support for custom user-defined compiler options, command-line arguments, and time and memory limits</li>
<li>Detailed execution results</li>
<li>Webhooks (HTTP callbacks)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For more information about these and other features, please <a href="https://ce.judge0.com" rel="nofollow">read the documentation</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Get Started</h2><a id="user-content-get-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Get Started" href="#get-started"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Feel free to start with the <a href="https://judge0.com/ce" rel="nofollow"><strong>FREE Basic Plan</strong></a> on RapidAPI or <a href="https://github.com/judge0/judge0/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#deployment-procedure">host it yourself</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can find our detailed plans and pricing <a href="https://judge0.com/#pricing" rel="nofollow">here</a>. So far our clients have run with us more than <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f3000945922c650888ee8235c6eb8aff039206c6db66a327b2a11a167424c1e1/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f656e64706f696e743f636f6c6f723d323138356430267374796c653d666c61742d7371756172652675726c3d68747470732533412532462532466a75646765302e636f6d253246737461746973746963732d6261646765"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f3000945922c650888ee8235c6eb8aff039206c6db66a327b2a11a167424c1e1/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f656e64706f696e743f636f6c6f723d323138356430267374796c653d666c61742d7371756172652675726c3d68747470732533412532462532466a75646765302e636f6d253246737461746973746963732d6261646765" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/endpoint?color=2185d0&amp;style=flat-square&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fjudge0.com%2Fstatistics-badge" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> programs.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why should you use Judge0 on RapidAPI?</h3><a id="user-content-why-should-you-use-judge0-on-rapidapi" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why should you use Judge0 on RapidAPI?" href="#why-should-you-use-judge0-on-rapidapi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Our infrastructure allows you to <strong>focus on building your product</strong> and forget about the know-how of maintaining and scaling Judge0.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Flavors</h2><a id="user-content-flavors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Flavors" href="#flavors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Judge0 comes in two flavors: <a href="https://judge0.com/ce" rel="nofollow">Judge0 CE</a> and <a href="https://judge0.com/extra-ce" rel="nofollow">Judge0 Extra CE</a>. They differ mostly in the <a href="#supported-languages">supported languages</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can find the source code for Judge0 CE on the <a href="https://github.com/judge0/judge0/tree/master"><code>master</code></a> branch, while you can find the source code for Judge0 Extra CE on the <a href="https://github.com/judge0/judge0/tree/extra"><code>extra</code></a> branch.</p>
<p dir="auto">Judge0 Extra CE is also available on <a href="https://judge0.com/extra-ce" rel="nofollow">RapidAPI</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Supported Languages</h2><a id="user-content-supported-languages" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Supported Languages" href="#supported-languages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Judge0 comes in two flavors: <a href="https://judge0.com/ce" rel="nofollow">Judge0 CE</a> and <a href="https://judge0.com/extra-ce" rel="nofollow">Judge0 Extra CE</a>. They differ mostly in the <a href="#supported-languages">supported languages</a>.</p>
